[[Zachary B.]] - My Survival Story<div align='center' style='font-size: 150%;'>\ Stuck on an Island\ </div> <div align='center' style='font-size: 120%;'>\ Addison J. [[Back->A-D]] \ </div> My name is Peyton. About 4 years ago my parents were traveling across the ocean on a boat called the Northwind. They were on there way to France, but they never made it. Everyone told me the boat must have sunk, everyone told me they were dead. I believed them, but I always kept hope that they were still alive. At one point in my life everything was perfect, but then the terrible news came. Two days after my parents were supposed to be in France, their ship had sunk. Rescuers searched and searched for the boat, but they never found it. Finally, the government made the conclusion that the boat must have been caught in a storm and sank. Ever since my parents passed away, my Grandma has been living with me in my house in Castle Heights. We live in the same house I grew up in with my parents, and it always seemed like an ordinary house. I go to the same school, and have all the same friends. Our house is beautiful, it looks right over a cliff, it has a garden, and even a pool! Then one day, I found a letter. The day was just like any other day. I woke up, got ready, ate breakfast, then went outside to water the flowers. When I got to the garden I found a letter on the ground. At first I was hesitant to pick it up, then after looking at it like it was an alien; I picked it up and read it. It read, “Our Dear Petyon, We need your help, we’re stuck on a magical island out in the middle of the sea. The garden you are standing in is a portal to this mysterious land. If you look in the envelope there should be some sort of object, maybe a bracelet or a crown. Whatever it is put it on and say, “ Leppell.” We don't want to put you in any harm, but you’re our only hope. I know your probably confused, but please do what the letter says. Help us come back home, Mother & Father” I read it over and over to make sure what I read was correct. Cautiously, I looked in the envelope to see a necklace with a key on it. This was it, this was the object they told me to put on. I glanced back at the house. What would grandmother do if she found out? Forcing those thoughts to the back of my head, I put the necklace around my neck and shouted, “ Leppell!” Suddenly, the ground started shaking, the petals started to fall from their stems and spin around me, it became extremely windy. All of the commotion became overwhelming. Before I knew it, everything was black. My eyes didn't want open, they didn’t want to open at all. Whatever just happened in my garden was crazy and weird! I was just fine with laying here for as long as I wanted. That feeling ended quickly when I felt water lightly touching me. I opened my eyes and looked around. At first I was very confused. Then I realized I was on some sort of island. Dusting the sand off of me, I stood up. There really wasn’t anything on the island. Just some big rocks, trees, and sand. I spent some time looking around. My stomach rumbled and I knew I needed to find some food. There were some coconuts that had fallen from a tree. I found a rock and cracked the coconut open. The coconut milk was refreshing, it seemed to cool me down. I looked around for more food and that’s when I saw a mysterious waterfall. Curious, I walked through it. Now I’ve had some pretty amazing moments in my life; but nothing could have topped what I saw right in front of me. There were my parents, sitting in something that looked like a fort. I ran to them with joy. I couldn’t believe it, they weren't dead! They were alive this whole time. They told me what happened. They said there was a storm, and they ended up on this island. When they were here they found out that they could send one message to one place in the entire world. Of course if they sent a random letter to the government, there was very little hope that the government was going to believe them. So they sent it to the garden, knowing I was going to get it. Thinking I was going to get something that would help them, they wrote me a letter hoping I would follow their instructions. “ So what do we do now?” I asked. “Well… how did you get here?” my father asked. “I just found a necklace with a key on it and put it on, then all of a sudden everything went black.” I replied. “Oh, we should’ve known!” my mother shouted. “This whole time we’ve been looking around for something that would let us leave, we discovered a box that had a lock on it. We thought it must have had something to do with freeing us because something inside of it was glowing.” my mother said pacing inside the little fort. “Well do you still have it?” I questioned. “ Yes!” she cried. “ Right over here. I kept it just in case.” I stared at it closely; it was glowing and something blue was inside. I took the necklace off, put the key in the lock, and stood back. All of a sudden the box flew open. A bright blue crystal sprang into the air. “Quick, grab it!” my mother yelled. I ran over to the box and reached for the crystal. It was like staring into the sun, it was so bright it could blind someone. “I have it!” I cried. “What do I do now?” Right after I said that, it started happening again. This time instead of flowers, sand was swirling around us. Again I thought I was stuck in a huge tornado. I looked over at my parents, the same thing was happening to them. It felt like I was having a panic attack. I looked around one more time; then everything went black. Memories started roaming through my head. It was like I was back at the island. All of a sudden the crystal wasn't working, the sand wasn’t spinning. There was some sort of hurricane. My mother was yelling my name over and over. A huge wave swept over her. “ No!” I yelled. I opened my eyes and I was panting. I was in my garden. “Peyton” my mother whispered. She and my father were hovering over me. “The hurricane swept you away!” I shouted looking over at my mother. “ No, No No … after you grabbed the crystal we all blacked out, but you didn’t come back so easily, it was just a bad dream. Everything is ok.” my mother reassured me. I took a breath of relief. “Now let's go find your Grandmother!” my mother said. We walked into the house. Apparently, time goes by a lot slower at home because my grandmother thought I was still in the garden. When she saw my parents she looked like a human finding a unicorn in the forest. They all hugged, cried, and hugged and cried some more. We explained everything that happened. Finally, we reported to everyone that they were found, and our family’s story spread throughout the nation. Over the past few years I've learned so much. After my parents died, I sulked for a long time. Eventually, I embraced what happened and learned to move. Mostly, I learned to never give up hope. I’m grateful that I found my parents and can’t wait for the adventure’s ahead. <div align='center' style='font-size: 150%;'>\ The Everfree\ </div> <div align='center' style='font-size: 120%;'>\ Addison M. [[Back->A-D]]\ </div> The sun was about to set and Alinna and Jade and their younger brother Alex were talking in their tent. “Have you ever heard of the Legend of the Everfree?” asked Jade. “No, what is that?” asked Alinna. “The Legend is a forest monster. I heard that It lives in the woods and comes out at night. Then at night, if the Everfree finds you it will take you back to it’s cave and never let you leave because it likes to collect people. The Everfree also leaves behind a trail of gold sparkles, which people like to try and find.” said Jade . “ We should go and look for this thing but we must not tell mom and dad because they will stop us” said Jade. “Are you guys sure?” said Alinna. “Yes” said Alex “This seems really scary and what if the everfree is true then we will be trapped forever?” said Alinna. They all agreed to go. Jade and Alinna go looking for the everfree with their brother Alex, because they wanted to see if the stories were true about the gold sparkles. They go to find the Everfree and don’t come back when morning rises. Their parents start to worry and while the kids are trying to find their way out of the Everfree traps and obstacles the two parents go looking for their three kids. One trap is wolves that are guarding the cave.They ran past the wolves who then chase them all through the woods . ”We are going to die!” said Alex with fear in his voice. “If we die I love you.” Alinna said to Jade. “I love you too.” Jade said . Running from the wolves was the scariest night of their lives by far. While running from the wolves they spotted a rope bridge that they maybe could cross. Then they could untie the bridge so the wolves could not chase them any more. As the three kids ran to the bridge they told Alex to get in front of them. As Alinna was about to cross the bridge the bridge broke and she was going to fall but Jade screamed “Jump!” So she took a leap of faith and jumped to the other side of the mountain. They all got to the other side safely and are so lucky Alinna made that jump. When they get to the campsite their parents were gone so they go looking for their parents. After hours of looking they don't find them In the deep dark woods. While they were looking for their parents they spot two or more Everfrees in the woods and one of them has their dad. They ran to their dad and he said that their mom was with the creature and they had to go get her. Going back to that cave would be very dangerous but they had to go back to get their mother. “Let’s make a plan.” said Dad. “I will grab a big log and use that as my bridge and I will cross and I will go to the cave and distract the everfree and while im doing that you three will cross and grab mom” said dad. Their plan worked and about an hour later they were all going back to the campsite. The lesson that the three kids learned was not to go looking for a weird creature in the woods even if there might be gold sparkles. <div align='center' style='font-size: 150%;'>\ Lost In The Amazon\ </div> <div align='center' style='font-size: 120%;'>\ Alex S. [[Back->A-D]]\ </div> One day John was flying over the amazon rainforest with his hunting partner Derek who he had met just before the trip and his pilot and friend Adam. When Derek and John got out of the helicopter adam flew away and they started to hunt. Everything was going smoothly, they got a lot of food and then went do the landing area where they would meet adam. The helicopter never came. As it started to get dark they built a shelter and ate some food and drank water. The next morning the helicopter still hadn't come. A few more days passed and there was still no sign of a helicopter anywhere. There was also no food both the men were starving the tried to eat plants but they never got any energy from it. Soon they were getting desperate and would go everywhere for food. Finally after almost two and a half weeks later John went down to the river and there were fish everywhere , he brought back as much as he could carry. As John gets back he sees Derek with a mushroom in his hands immediately Derek charges him and John runs out of the way dropping all the fish Derek eats all the fish then looks over at John then John gets his gun and Derek backs off. For a day Derek was a cannibal trying to eat John but after Derek finished digesting the mushroom he returned to normal. Then one day John and Derek decide to go and try to Signal a helicopter or a plane to save them but as they were walking and they found a helicopter that looked just like the one that they took as they walked closer they found that it was their helicopter. It had run out of fuel and couldn't perform an autorotation which is a helicopter using the wind to keep the blades spinning and land. They also found Adam's Body it was pale and leathery and they buried him beside the helicopter. But they also found other survival supplies like food, water and a tent they also found radio supplies that would help them contact another helicopter or plane. After returning to camp they decided to try and Signal somebody after about an hour of nothing but static they finally heard somebody on the other side of the radio as soon as they heard that they told the person their coordinates and they said they'd be on their way. In in the end they were rescued John had a broken leg and Derek had PTSD but they were both alive. They're both going to live full lives and go on more hunting trips together always returning to the same camp to spend the night. <div align='center' style='font-size: 150%;'>\ The Road Trip\ </div> <div align='center' style='font-size: 120%;'>\ Alexa S. But she also had a lot of her own hobbies like swimming,going to the beach and she just loves wild life. She was trying to calm Emma down then Viot got up and started looking around to see if she recognized anything, but to her disappointment she knew nothing. They were in the middle of nowhere and there wasn't any cars driving either. “Oh no” “ what am I supposed to do now”? Viot walked to the driver's seat and her mom wasn't there and she picked up her moms phone and she tried to turn it on to call 911 but it did not work. “no ,no,no’’ Viot said clearly trying not to panic. Violet started to walk toward the beach, and on the side was a forest. Violet looked around.The place was deserted. “Why can't there be people here, come on it's a beach there is supposed to be people here.’’ Violet said with a mixture of worry,sadness,and frustration. Violet walked to the forest and started to build a fire. She went to a lot of survival camps and knew how to build a fire,make a tent and normal survival stuff but she never knew that it was actually going to happen. She spread out a blanket on the ground and let Emma play with her toys there. She started to look around to see if there was anyone was there or if there was a plane in the sky that could rescue them. As the days passed Violet had already built a little tent out of mud and sticks they were running out of food so Violet stopped eating so Emma can eat and be strong. Emma was already learning to walk so she wanted to walk everywear, so Violet decided that they would take a walk to the beach and Emma would play and splash in the water. [[Back->A-D]]\ </div> <div align='center' style='font-size: 150%;'>\ Chapter 1\ </div> Im Jason, Jason Roberts. I am 12 years old. I'm going to a baseball game in England for the championships. I snatched her blue and pink scarf from the shelf and tip-toed out back into my room. I reached into my back jeans pocket and pulled out the lighter I stole from the gas station hours earlier. I squished myself far into the corner trying to keep out of the searing flames reach.
